namespace = colonial_goods
namespace = development_goods
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.1
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.1"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			AND = {
				continent = europe
				NOT = {
					superregion = scandinavian_superregion
				}
			}
			AND = {
				continent = oceania
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = wheat
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ivory
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = tea
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cinnamon
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = clove
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pepper
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = coffee
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cotton
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = sugar
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = tobacco
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = opium
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cacao
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cheese
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = carmine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = lumber
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.7
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = livestock
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = olive
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = wheat
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.2
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.2"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					superregion = east_africa_superregion
					superregion = west_africa_superregion
					superregion = north_africa_superregion
					region = egypt_region
				}
			}
			AND = {
				continent = oceania
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								AND = {
									OR = {
										superregion = east_africa_superregion
										superregion = west_africa_superregion

										region = egypt_region
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}

							colonial_parent = {

									AND = {

									}

		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
	}

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.3
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.3"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			AND = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						continent = southeast_asia
						continent = indian_continent
						continent = east_asia
						continent = central_asia
						continent = north_asia
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					region = east_siberia_region
					region = west_siberia_region
				}
			}
			AND = {
				continent = oceania
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								AND = {
									OR = {
										continent = southeast_asia
										continent = indian_continent
										continent = east_asia
										continent = central_asia
										continent = north_asia
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									AND = {
										OR = {
											continent = southeast_asia
											continent = indian_continent
											continent = east_asia
											continent = central_asia
											continent = north_asia
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = rice
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine

				}
				set_variable = {

					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = rice
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.4
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.4"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			continent = north_america
			continent = south_america
			AND = {
				continent = oceania
				OR = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							owner = {
								is_colonial_nation = no
							}
							owner = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = north_america
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							owner = {
								is_colonial_nation = yes
							}
							owner = {
								colonial_parent = {
									capital_scope = {
										continent = north_america
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							owner = {
								is_colonial_nation = no
							}
							owner = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = south_america
								}
							}
						}

		}

		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
	}
	immediate = {

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.5
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.5"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			AND = {
				trade_goods = slaves
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wine = 1
		}
		OR = {
			region = south_africa_region
			AND = {
				superregion = west_america_superregion
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			owner = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = langue_d_oil
					culture_group = langue_d_oc
					culture_group = iberian
					culture_group = latin
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = wine

				value = 0
			}

					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize

				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good

				limit = {
					trade_goods = olive
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = wine
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.12
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.12"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			region = east_siberia_region
			region = west_siberia_region
			region = great_plains_region
			superregion = north_america_superregion
			AND = {
				continent = north_america
				OR = {
					superregion = north_america_superregion
					region = great_lakes_region
				}
			}
			region = north_oceanea_region
			region = south_oceanea_region
			region = mississippi_region
			AND = {
				superregion = west_america_superregion
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = wood_flats
					has_terrain = wood_hills
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
				}
			}
			has_terrain = taiga
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = lumber
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good

				}
			}
			if = {

				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = brazil
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.14
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.14"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			continent = indian_continent
			AND = {
				continent = southeast_asia
				OR = {
					superregion = east_indies_superregion
					region = malaya_region
				}
			}
			continent = oceania
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = sandal
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet

					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.17
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.17"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			AND = {
				trade_goods = slaves
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				superregion = east_africa_superregion
				OR = {
					region = somalia_region
					region = east_africa_region
					region = madagascar_region
				}
			}
			continent = indian_continent
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 4
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = pepper
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ivory
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = tea
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cinnamon
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = clove
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pepper
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = coffee
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cotton
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = sugar
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = tobacco
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = opium
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cacao
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = cheese
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = carmine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = lumber
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.7
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = livestock
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = olive
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = pepper
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.18
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.18"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		AND = {
			continent = southeast_asia
			OR = {
				superregion = east_indies_superregion
				region = malaya_region
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = clove
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}

					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}

			if = {

					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}

			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5

				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}

				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat

					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese

						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee

				}

			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = olive
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = nutmeg
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.20
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.20"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		has_port = yes

			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.65

	}

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.22
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.22"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act
			}
		}
		OR = {
			region = central_africa_region
			AND = {
				superregion = east_africa_superregion
				OR = {
					region = somalia_region
					region = east_africa_region
					region = madagascar_region
				}
			}
			region = south_africa_region
			AND = {
				continent = sub_sahara
				OR = {
					region = west_africa_region
					region = mali_region
					region = volta_region
					region = manding_region
					region = central_africa_region
					region = gulf_of_nigeria_region
					region = coastal_kongo_region
					region = inland_kongo_region
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {

			change_trade_goods = slaves

				}

					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}

					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = carmine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}

				limit = {

				}

				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {

					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = slaves
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.23
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.23"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		always = no
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			trade_goods = slaves
		}
		NOT = {
			trade_goods = gems
		}
		NOT = {
			trade_goods = gold
		}
		NOT = {
			trade_goods = silver
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = eventcolonial_goods.23
		}
		NOT = {
			base_tax = 5
		}
		OR = {
			region = central_africa_region
			AND = {
				superregion = east_africa_superregion
				OR = {
					region = somalia_region
					region = east_africa_region
					region = madagascar_region
				}
			}
			region = south_africa_region
			AND = {
				continent = sub_sahara
				OR = {
					region = west_africa_region
					region = mali_region
					region = volta_region
					region = manding_region
					region = central_africa_region
					region = gulf_of_nigeria_region
					region = coastal_kongo_region
					region = inland_kongo_region
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}

					}

									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = slaves
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				limit = {

				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {

					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				}

				}

			if = {
				limit = {

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.24
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.24"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			OR = {
				region = southeast_america_region
				region = mississippi_region
				region = carribeans_region
				region = texas_region
				area = central_valley_area
				area = sao_paolo_area
			}
		}
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
			cotton = 1
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
					has_terrain = wood_highlands
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
					has_terrain = grass_highlands
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats

					has_terrain = desert_flats

			colonysize = 300

			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}

		years = 5

					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = cotton
	}
	after = {
		set_province_flag = new_good_set
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.25
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.25"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				region = southeast_america_region
				region = mississippi_region
				region = carribeans_region
				region = texas_region
				area = central_valley_area
				area = sao_paolo_area
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				cotton = 1
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
					has_terrain = wood_highlands
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
					has_terrain = grass_highlands
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = jungle_flats
					has_terrain = jungle_hills
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert_flats
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			has_climate = arctic
			has_climate = arid
			has_winter = severe_winter
			has_winter = normal_winter
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			region = carribeans_region
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = cotton
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}

	trigger = {

		}

			}

				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = tobacco
	}
	after = {
		set_province_flag = new_good_set
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.27
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.27"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				region = southeast_america_region
				region = northeast_america_region
				area = cuba_area
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				tobacco = 1
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_climate = arid
				NOT = {
					has_terrain = grass_flats
				}
			}
			has_winter = severe_winter
			has_terrain = tundra
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = shrub_flats
					has_terrain = shrub_hills
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert_flats
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = tobacco
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ivory
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good

				}

	id = colonial_goods.28
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.28"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		has_climate = tropical
		OR = {
			superregion = eastern_south_america_superregion
			region = carribeans_region
		}
		owner = {
			sugar = 1
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = grass_hills
					has_terrain = shrub_hills
					has_terrain = wood_hills
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = jungle_hills
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
				}
			}

			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = jungle_flats
					has_terrain = jungle_hills
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert_flats

					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}

				OR = {
					has_terrain = grass_flats

				}
				OR = {
					region = steppes_region
					superregion = central_asia_superregion
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5

			factor = 2

					AND = {

						}

							}
						}
					}

				}

					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = sugar
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					continent = north_america
					continent = south_america
				}
			}
			AAA = {
				change_variable = {
					which = american_sugar
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		set_province_flag = new_good_set
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.29
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.29"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		has_climate = tropical
		OR = {
			superregion = eastern_south_america_superregion
			region = carribeans_region
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				sugar = 1
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			has_winter = severe_winter
			has_winter = normal_winter
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = grass_hills
					has_terrain = shrub_hills
					has_terrain = wood_hills
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = jungle_hills
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains

				}
			}

					has_terrain = forest_highlands
					has_terrain = wood_highlands

					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = jungle_flats
					has_terrain = jungle_hills
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert_flats
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = grass_flats
					has_terrain = grass_hills
				}
				OR = {
					region = steppes_region
					superregion = central_asia_superregion
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = sugar
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}

				limit = {

				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = olive
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = coffee
	}
	after = {
		set_province_flag = new_good_set
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.31
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.31"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		OR = {
			region = peru_region
			region = carribeans_region
			region = colombia_region
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				coffee = 1
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			has_terrain = tundra
			has_terrain = taiga
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
				}
			}
			has_climate = arctic
			has_winter = severe_winter
			has_winter = normal_winter
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = coffee
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ivory
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = tea
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6

				set_variable = {

	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.32"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {

			dip_tech = 24

			region = peru_region
			region = carribeans_region

					trade_goods = olive
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = brazil
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = nutmeg
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = indigo
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = potatoes
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = palm_date
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = incense
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = slaves
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = cacao
	}
	after = {
		set_province_flag = new_good_set
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.33
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.33"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		OR = {
			region = peru_region
			region = carribeans_region
			region = colombia_region
			region = central_america_region
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				cacao = 1
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			has_terrain = tundra
			has_terrain = taiga
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_flats
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
				}
			}
			has_climate = arctic
			has_winter = severe_winter
			has_winter = normal_winter
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = cacao
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = millet
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = rice
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wine
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wax
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wool
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = pearls
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = hemp
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fish
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = fur
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 2.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ivory
				}
				set_variable = {

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.34
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.34"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			AND = {
				trade_goods = slaves
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
		AND = {
			continent = sub_sahara
			OR = {
				region = west_africa_region
				region = mali_region
				region = volta_region
				region = manding_region
				region = central_africa_region
				region = gulf_of_nigeria_region
				region = coastal_kongo_region
				region = inland_kongo_region
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}

					value = 0.5
				}

				}
				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = grain_province
			clr_province_flag = plantation_goods
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "OPT.VERYWELL"
		change_trade_goods = palm
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.38
	title = "NEWS_FROM_COL"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.38"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		trade_goods = unknown
		OR = {
			AND = {
				owner = {
					is_colonial_nation = no
				}
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						continent = europe
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					is_colonial_nation = yes
				}
				owner = {
					colonial_parent = {
						capital_scope = {
							continent = europe
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = grass_hills
					has_terrain = shrub_hills
					has_terrain = wood_hills
					has_terrain = forest_hills
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = jungle_hills
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
					has_terrain = wood_highlands
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
					has_terrain = grass_highlands
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			region = la_plata_region
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = livestock
			set_variable = {
				which = price_of_rural_good
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = wheat

				}

				}

				}

				limit = {
					trade_goods = maize

				set_variable = {
					which = price_of_rural_good
					value = 0.5

			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				}

					value = 1.6

			if = {

				limit = {

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.40
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 24
		}
		OR = {
			region = colombia_region
			continent = indian_continent
			area = oaxaca_area
			area = zapotec_area
		}
		owner = {
			carmine = 1
		}
		NOT = {
			AAA = {
				check_variable = {
					which = world_dye_supply
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine

		}

			has_climate = arid
