		OR = {
			region = colombia_region
			continent = indian_continent
			area = oaxaca_area
			area = zapotec_area
		}
		NOT = {
			AAA = {
				check_variable = {
					which = world_dye_supply
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			has_climate = arid
			has_climate = arctic
			has_winter = normal_winter
			has_winter = severe_winter
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.41"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_trade_goods = carmine

			}

province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.42
	trigger = {
		is_year = 1650
		OR = {
			AND = {
				superregion = japan_superregion
			}
			area = assam_area
			region = la_plata_region
		}
		owner = {
			tea = 1
		}
		NOT = {
			AAA = {
				check_variable = {
					which = world_tea_supply
					value = 5
				}
			}

			trade_goods = unknown

			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
					has_terrain = wood_highlands
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
					has_terrain = grass_highlands
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = shrub_flats
					has_terrain = shrub_hills
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert_flats
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			has_climate = arid
			has_winter = normal_winter
			has_winter = severe_winter
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 300
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {

			}
		}
		OR = {
			trade_goods = unknown
			trade_goods = fish
			trade_goods = livestock
			trade_goods = lumber
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			trade_goods = wine
			trade_goods = wool
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_mountains
					has_terrain = wood_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = grass_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = alpine_tundra
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = forest_highlands
					has_terrain = wood_highlands
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands
					has_terrain = grass_highlands
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = shrub_flats
					has_terrain = shrub_hills
					has_terrain = shrub_mountains
					has_terrain = shrub_highlands

			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert_flats
					has_terrain = desert_hills
					has_terrain = desert_mountains
					has_terrain = desert_highlands
				}
			}
			has_climate = arid
			has_winter = normal_winter
			has_winter = severe_winter
		}
		OR = {
			colonysize = 500
			is_city = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = new_good_set
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = no
						}
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							is_colonial_nation = yes
						}
						owner = {
							colonial_parent = {
								capital_scope = {
									continent = europe
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}
				set_variable = {

					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trade_goods = ebony
				}
				set_variable = {

					value = 2.5
				}

				}

			if = {

					OR = {
						trade_goods = wheat
						trade_goods = millet
						trade_goods = rice
						trade_goods = maize
						trade_goods = fish
						trade_goods = potatoes
						trade_goods = livestock
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = grain_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = cheese
						trade_goods = olive
						trade_goods = palm
						trade_goods = palm_date
						trade_goods = wax
						trade_goods = wine
						trade_goods = tea
						trade_goods = cinnamon
						trade_goods = clove
						trade_goods = pepper
						trade_goods = coffee
						trade_goods = cotton
						trade_goods = sugar
						trade_goods = tobacco
						trade_goods = opium
						trade_goods = cacao
						trade_goods = carmine
						trade_goods = nutmeg
						trade_goods = hemp
						trade_goods = indigo
						trade_goods = lumber
						trade_goods = ebony
						trade_goods = incense
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = plantation_goods
			}
			set_province_flag = had_event_coffee
			AAA = {
				change_variable = {
					which = yemen_coffee
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = colonial_goods.103
	title = "EVTNAMEcolonial_goods.103"
	desc = "EVTDESCcolonial_goods.103"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			sanaa_area = {
				trade_goods = coffee
			}
			yemen_area = {
				trade_goods = coffee
			}
		}
		owner = {
			dip_tech = 23
			NOT = {
				religion = coptic
			}
		}
		OR = {
			area = sidamo_area
			area = hadiya_area
			area = ifat_area
		}
		OR = {

				}

	}

		years = 5

province_event = {
	id = development_goods.100
	title = "EVTNAMEdevelopment_goods.100"
	desc = "EVTDESCdevelopment_goods.100"
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		province_id = 118
		is_year = 1440
		owner = {
			adm_tech = 15
			NOT = {
				is_at_war = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = mined_goods
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
